## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population size P, which is the canonical form of population dynamics ODEs. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth mechanisms such as logistic, Allee, or predator-prey effects.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent unlimited growth)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth rate decreases logarithmically with population)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population threshold)
- Allee effect (weak): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 + P) (reduced growth at low density without extinction threshold)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (saturating per-capita growth rate)
- Cubic population dynamics: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (polynomial density dependence)
- Time-varying Malthusian: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (exponential growth with time-varying rate)
- Logistic with time-dependent capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t)) (carrying capacity changes over time)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (growth as balance between anabolism and catabolism)
- Harvesting model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (logistic growth with constant harvesting)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (generalized asymmetric sigmoid growth)
- Periodic forcing: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (logistic growth with seasonal variation)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear proportionality to P (dP_dt ~ c*P) indicates density-independent exponential growth regime
- Quadratic term in P (dP_dt ~ c0*P - c1*P^2) indicates pairwise competition or logistic-type carrying capacity
- Cubic term in P (dP_dt ~ P*(P-a)*(K-P)) indicates Allee effect with both lower and upper critical densities
- Logarithmic dependence on P (dP_dt ~ P*log(K/P)) indicates Gompertz-type asymmetric growth near carrying capacity
- Rational dependence on P (dP_dt ~ P/(1+cP)) indicates saturating resource uptake or interference competition
- Multiplicative time-population coupling (dP_dt ~ f(t)*g(P)) indicates separable environmental forcing on intrinsic dynamics
- Sign change in dP_dt at specific P values indicates equilibrium points (stable or unstable fixed points of the ODE)
- Fractional power of P (dP_dt ~ P^c with 0<c<1) indicates surface-area-to-volume scaling in organism growth
- Sinusoidal time dependence in growth rate indicates seasonal or periodic environmental forcing
